                                                                                                                                   CONVERSATION I.
                                                                                                                                      INTRODUCTION.
Generated for acobblah (University of Michigan) on 2015-08-10 15:08 GMT / http://hdl.handle.net/2027/hvd.32044102874120
                                                                                                                              FATHER — CHAHZ.ES — EMMA.
                                                                                                                            FATHER. In pursuing       our course
                                                                                                                          of natural and experimental      philo
                                                                                                                          sophy,   we shall   now proceed with
                                                                                                                          that branch of science which is called
                                                                                                                          Hydrostatics.
                                                                                                                            Emma.      That is a difficult word ;
                                                                                                                          what are we to understand by it?
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                            Father.    Almost all the technical
                                                                                                                          terms    made use  of in science are
                                                                                                                          either   Greek, or derived from'the
                                                                                                                          Greek Language.     The word hydro-
                                                                                                                            vol. m.            B

                                                                                                                          2               HYDROSTATICS.
                                                                                                                          statics is formed of two Greek words,
                                                                                                                          which signify water, and the science
                                                                                                                          which considers the weight          of     bodies.
                                                                                                                          But hydrostatics,       as a branch   of natu
                                                                                                                          ral philosophy, treats of the nature,
                                                                                                                          gravity, pressure, and motion of fluids
                                                                                                                          in  general; and of the methods of
                                                                                                                          Aveighing solids in them.
                                                                                                                               Charles.    Is    this an important part
Generated for acobblah (University of Michigan) on 2015-08-10 15:08 GMT / http://hdl.handle.net/2027/hvd.32044102874120
                                                                                                                          of knowledge      ?
                                                                                                                               Father.     Taken      in this extensive
                                                                                                                          sense, it yields to none as to its real
                                                                                                                          importance.           And   the    experiments
                                                                                                                          which    I   shall show you are curious
                                                                                                                          and highly amusing.
                                                                                                                               Emma.       Shall we be able to repeat
                                                                                                                          tliem ourselves?
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                               Father,     Most of them you will,
                                                                                                                          provided        you are     very    careful     in
                                                                                                                          using the instruments, almost all of
                                                                                                                          which are made of glass.               I    ought

                                                                                                                                    DEFINITION OF FLUIDS.                          3
                                                                                                                          to tell you that many writers divide
                                                                                                                          this subject into two distinct parts,
                                                                                                                          viz. hydrostatics and hydraulics;                       the
                                                                                                                          latter relates particularly to the mo
                                                                                                                          tion of water through pipes, conduits,
                                                                                                                          &c.
                                                                                                                               In   these conversations,             I  shall pay
                                                                                                                          no    regard         to     this       distinction, but
                                                                                                                          shall, under the general title of hy
Generated for acobblah (University of Michigan) on 2015-08-10 15:08 GMT / http://hdl.handle.net/2027/hvd.32044102874120
                                                                                                                          drostatics, describe the properties                      of
                                                                                                                          all fluids,       but       principally         those    of
                                                                                                                          water     ;   explaining, as we go on, the
                                                                                                                          motions         of    it,    whether           in   pipes,
                                                                                                                          pumps, siphons, engines                   of different
                                                                                                                          kinds, fountains, &c.                   Do you know
                                                                                                                          what      a   fluid is?                                  ;
                                                                                                                               Charles.    I        know how to distinguish
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                          a   fluid from       a     solid   :   water and wine
                                                                                                                          are fluids, but why they are so called
                                                                                                                          I   cannot tell.
                                                                                                                                                      B  2

                                                                                                                          4        v    HYDROSTATICS.
                                                                                                                              Father.     A
                                                                                                                                         fluid is generally de
                                                                                                                          fined as a body, the parts of which
                                                                                                                          readily yield to any impression, and in
                                                                                                                          yielding are easily moved among each
                                                                                                                          other.
                                                                                                                              Emma.       But this definition   does
                                                                                                                          not notice the wetting of other bodies
                                                                                                                          brought into contact with a fluid.      If
                                                                                                                          I put my     fingers into water or milk, a
Generated for acobblah (University of Michigan) on 2015-08-10 15:08 GMT / http://hdl.handle.net/2027/hvd.32044102874120
                                                                                                                          part of it adheres to them, and they
                                                                                                                          are said to be wet.
                                                                                                                              Father.     Every accurate definition
                                                                                                                          must mark the qualities of all the indi
                                                                                                                          vidual things defined by it : now there
                                                                                                                          are many fluids which have not the
                                                                                                                          property of wetting the hand when
                                                                                                                          plunged into them.     The air we
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                          breathe is a fluid, the parts of which
                                                                                                                          yield to the least pressure, but it does
                                                                                                                          not adhere to the bodies surrounded
                                                                                                                          by it like water.

                                                                                                                                    DEFINITION OF FLUIDS.                5
                                                                                                                                Emma.      Air, however, is      so differ
                                                                                                                          ent from water, that, in this respect,
                                                                                                                          they will scarcely admit of compa
                                                                                                                          rison.
                                                                                                                                Charles.    I have sometimes dipped
                                                                                                                          my finger into a cup of quicksilver,
                                                                                                                          but none of the fluid came away with
                                                                                                                          it.
                                                                                                                                Father.    You   are right       and hence
Generated for acobblah (University of Michigan) on 2015-08-10 15:08 GMT / http://hdl.handle.net/2027/hvd.32044102874120
                                                                                                                                                             ;
                                                                                                                          you will find that some writers on na
                                                                                                                          tural philosophy distinguish between
                                                                                                                          fluids and liquids.        Air, quicksilver,
                                                                                                                          and melted metals, are fluids, but not
                                                                                                                          liquids : while water, milk, beer, wine,
                                                                                                                          oil, spirits, &c. are fluids and liquids.
                                                                                                                              Charles. Are we then to under
                                                                                                                          stand, that liquids are known by the
Public Domain, Google-digitized / http://www.hathitrust.org/access_use#pd-google
                                                                                                                          property of adhering to different
                                                                                                                          substances which         are   immersed        in
                                                                                                                          them ?

                                                                                                                            FA THER. Here is a glass               model

                                                                                                                          kind of lid or trap-door, that opens one
